<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ратный.html>ра́тный</a> (26450)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рать.html>рать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ratʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> military, combat

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>ра́т<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a.

***ратовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ратовать.html>ратова́ть</a> (23042)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рать.html>рать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ratʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ратовать.html>ра́товать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rátovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fight <i>(for)</i>, to stand up <i>(for)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to declaim <i>(against)</i>, to inveigh <i>(against)</i></li></ol>

<p><b>ра́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать</b>

***ратуша.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ратуша.html>ра́туша</a> (24465)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:ратуша.html>ра́туша</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ratuša</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">ratusz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">rāthūs</i>; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Rathaus</i>. Polish <span class="IPA">/ʃ/</span> replaced Middle High German <i>s</i> because at the time, this letter was pronounced as <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/apicoalveolar" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:apicoalveolar">apicoalveolar</a> <span class="IPA">/s̺/</span> (with a weak hushing sound, similar to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Castilian_Spanish" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Castilian Spanish">Castilian Spanish</a>) and was distinct from the letter written <i>z</i>, pronounced as <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/laminoalveolar" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:laminoalveolar">laminoalveolar</a> <span class="IPA">/s/</span> (with a strong hissing sound, similar to English).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ратуша.html>ра́туша</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rátuša</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ратуша.html>ра́туши</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ратуша.html>ра́туши</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ратуша.html>ра́туш</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> administrative body of a city or township</li>
<li>town hall</li></ol>

***рать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рать.html>рать</a> (19278)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ortь</i>. Related to <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">реть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">retĭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">quarrel, competition</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">ऋति</i> <span href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">ऋतीयते</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ṛtīyate</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to quarrel, to hate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" for further descendants)

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рать.html>рать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ratʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рать.html>ра́ти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рать.html>ра́ти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рать.html>ра́тей</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ратный.html>ра́тный</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic or folk poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> army, host, array</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic or folk poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> battle, war</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рафинированный.html>рафини́рованный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rafinírovannyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рафини́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rafinírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рафини́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rafinírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рафинированный.html>рафини́рованный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rafinírovannyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)рафини́рованнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)рафини́рованней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>purified, refined
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b>рефини́рованный</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сахар.html>са́хар</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>refinírovannyj</b> sáxar</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>refined</b> sugar</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pure, genuine</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> overly refined, recherché</li>
<li>refined, exquisite, sophisticated
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:рафинированный.html>рафини́рованный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вкус.html>вкус</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rafinírovannyj</b> vkus</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>refined</b> taste</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рвавший.html>рва́вший</a> (2882)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рвавший.html>рва́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rvávšij</span>)

***рвануть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рвануть.html>рвану́ть</a> (3342)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рвать.html>рвать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ану́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-anútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рвануть.html>рвану́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rvanútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to tear</li>
<li>to jerk, to tug</li>
<li>to start with a jerk, to get off with a jerk</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dash, to rush, to race, to scurry, to spurt; <i>(car)</i> to speed, to tear off, to zip, to zoom</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take flight, to take to one's heels, to whip off, to whip away, to dash off</li>
<li>to blow up, to blast</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ров.html>рва</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ну́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 3b.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-рв-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-а-ну</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рвануться.html>рвану́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rvanútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ров.html>рва</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ну́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 3b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:рваться.html>рва́ться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-рв-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-а-ну</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***рвать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рвать.html>рвать</a> (2882)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">ръвати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rŭvati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*rъvàti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рвать.html>рвать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порвать.html>порва́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разорвать.html>разорва́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изорвать.html>изорва́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сорвать.html>сорва́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рвануть.html>рвану́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tear (rend)</li>
<li>to tear apart
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неисправный.html>неиспра́вный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:принтер.html>при́нтер</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рвать.html>рвёт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бумага.html>бума́гу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ничто.html>ничего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:печатать.html>печа́тает</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Neisprávnyj príntɛr tólʹko <b>rvjót</b> bumágu i ničevó ne pečátajet.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">A broken printer only tears the paper apart and doesn't print anything.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to tear out</li>
<li>to break</li>
<li>to break up, to break off (a relationship)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рвать.html>рвёт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уезжать.html>уезжа́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> далёкий <a href = vnd.unilang:город.html>го́род</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>rvjót</b> so vsem i ujezžájet v daljókij górod.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He breaks everything off and leaves for a faraway town.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to pick, to pluck <i>flowers or fruits</i>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сорвать.html>сорва́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sorvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рвать.html>рвать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырвать.html>вы́рвать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to vomit, to puke, to feel sick <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">impersonal, the person vomiting is the object</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Её</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рвать.html>рвёт</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jejó <b>rvjót</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">She <b>is vomiting</b>. / She is feeling sick.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рвать.html>рва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рваться.html>рва́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rvátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порваться.html>порва́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разорваться.html>разорва́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">изорва́ться</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сорваться.html>сорва́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to break, to burst, to be torn</li>
<li>to strive, to long, to be dying to (to do something)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рвать.html>рвать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b>рво́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>та</a></b>

***рдеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рдеть.html>рдеть</a> (29414)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">ръдѣти сѧ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rŭděti sę</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*rъděti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рдеть.html>рдеть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rdetʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">зарде́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated or poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to redden, to blush</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:реабилитировать.html>реабилити́ровать</a> (13163)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">réhabiliter</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>
<ol><li>to rehabilitate, to exonerate
